<div class="wp-block-column is-vertically-aligned-center is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Who is the Organized Adventurer?</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-medium-font-size">I&#8217;m Sarah, and I&#8217;ve spent the last decade traveling around the world to all 7 continents and over 70 countries with my husband, Tim. Whether you&#8217;re taking a <a href="https://organizedadventurer.com/destinations/">year-long round-the-world trip</a> or a weekend getaway in the <a href="https://organizedadventurer.com/category/north-america/united-states/">United States</a>, and everything in between, let our first-hand experience guide your next adventure! </p>
</div>
</div>
